void dfs(int x, int y){ maxi = max(x, maxi), maxj = max(y, maxj), mini = min(x, mini), minj = min(y, minj), cnt++, a[x][y] = false; for(int i=1; i<=4; i++){ int xx = x + fx[i], yy = y + fy[i];
